Current Affairs Commentary

The Significance of Expanding Air Routes in the Pacific Ocean 17

— Hua

Recently, there have been several important pieces of news regarding the expansion of air routes in the Pacific Ocean. These are worthy of attention: (1) The trans-Pacific air route, which has been in operation for over a year and is managed by Pan American Airways, will conduct a full-line test flight next month. Formal service is expected to begin in January next year. The route starts in San Francisco and temporarily ends in Macau. In the future, it may extend to Hong Kong, and eventually hopes to reach ports in southern China. (2) On the 13th of this month, the US authorities announced the incorporation of Jarvis, Baker, and Howland Islands in the South Pacific into US territory, preparing to open an air route from Hawaii to Australia, connecting the British and American air routes. These three islands will serve as important transit stations. (3) Earlier this month, Mr. Smith, the British aviation supervisor, came to the Far East to inspect the bases of the Royal Air Force. He stated that Britain would establish a huge civilian and military aviation base in Hong Kong. On the 24th, the Royal Air Force aircraft Dorade successfully flew from Penang to Hong Kong, setting a record of twelve hours. It is said that test flights will continue. It is likely that a branch line of the British-Australian air route will be established from Singapore to Hong Kong in the near future.

From the perspective of the development of world transportation, the above news is all welcome. In the vast world, human beings are scattered across several landmasses, separated by vast oceans. This natural barrier is one of the reasons for the separation between human beings. Thanks to the development of science, humans have finally acquired the means to transcend the oceans and control the wind in the sky. This should be an important boost in promoting international cooperation and the ideal of human harmony. But the current reality seems to be quite different. What frightens the world today is the crisis of war caused by hostility between humans and suspicion between nations. Currently, the scientific tools of many countries are not working for the ideal of peace, but are instead listening to the command of the god of war. In the winds and clouds over the Pacific Ocean, there has suddenly been a surge in the activity of these many aircraft. While we certainly hold great respect for those warriors who conquer nature, at the same time, we cannot help but have some doubts about the meaning of this expansion of air routes.

In recent years, the shores of the Pacific Ocean have been filled with the smoke of war. All aviation activities during this period do not seem to be able to escape military relations. The islands through which the United States established a trans-Pacific air route have mostly been placed under the administration of the military. The British air routes to the Far East are also run by the Royal Air Force. After reading the article "Japan Under the Wings of Aircraft" in the August issue of American Mercury magazine this year, we know that the sharp increase in Japan's military budget since 1931 is also related to the development of military aviation. Currently, competition among countries' air routes in the Pacific has triggered an important role in politics and diplomacy. Pan American Airways is still keeping the routes and destinations of its Pacific air routes a closely guarded secret because of "diplomatic subtleties." At the same time, according to the Associated Press, European countries are also trying to consolidate air transportation between Europe and Asia because of the expansion of US air routes. For example, Britain plans to expand its air routes to China, and France has allowed British air routes to pass through Annam, allowing its air routes to have a stopover point in Hong Kong and reach China from Hanoi. These are significant signs.

It is extremely noteworthy that the great powers hope to make our country the terminus of their air routes. The winds and clouds over the Pacific Ocean originally centered on the China problem. Now that the air routes in the Pacific Ocean are actively extending to the coast of our country, the ambition of the great powers to seize control of our country's gateway is even more evident. In the future great explosion in the Pacific, our country will be entirely under the threat of other people's wings. As it stands now, our northern and eastern coastal skies are often roamed arbitrarily by foreign aircraft. Our country's air sovereignty has been completely destroyed, which has shown the signs of future disasters. Because of the expansion of the great powers' air routes in the Pacific, and thinking of the crisis hidden here, I especially raise this issue for the authorities and people of our country to pay close attention to.

Italy Accepts British Invitation to Participate in Naval Conference; Japanese Representatives Designated 18

(Rome) A Foreign Ministry spokesman stated today that Italy will accept Britain's invitation to participate in the naval conference to be held in London on December 2. (National News Agency dispatch, 25th)

(Tokyo) The Japanese government's reply to Britain will be submitted to the cabinet meeting on the 29th and issued immediately after approval. Its content roughly states that Japan is pleased to participate in the arms reduction conference stipulated in the Washington and London treaties, and believes that the ideal is to have armaments that do not invade or threaten other countries, and to exchange views with various countries in order to achieve a fair purpose. (Japan Associated Press dispatch, 26th)

(Tokyo) After the Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs received the British government's formal invitation to the arms reduction conference yesterday, it immediately consulted with the Ministry of the Navy to organize a plenipotentiary delegation. As a result, the list of Japanese delegates was decided as follows: Chairman and Plenipotentiary, Admiral Nagano Osami; Plenipotentiary, Ambassador to France Sato Naotake; Expert Commissioners, Navy Colonel Iwashita Hotaro, Foreign Ministry Secretary Yamagata Kiyoshi, Navy Colonel Satoda Toshichiro; Secretary General, Counselor to the United Kingdom Fujii Keinosuke; Attendants, Navy Secretary Enomoto Shigeji, Foreign Ministry Official Ando Yoshira, Navy Lieutenant Colonel Nishida Masao (Japan Associated Press dispatch, 26th)

East African War Enters Fourth Week; Italian and Abyssinian Armies Remain Silent; Ships Shuttle Back and Forth as Italy Continues to Reinforce Troops; Abyssinian Imperial Guard Defends the Main Road to the Capital 19

Asmara, regarding the military situation, the Italian army in the north is in a position to advance or retreat as it chooses. However, judging from the current situation, whether the Italian army will continue its operations cannot be determined solely from a military perspective. In other words, it still depends on diplomatic relations. (National Telegram, 25th)

(Rome) The war in Abyssinia has now entered its fourth week, with both sides remaining silent. Only the sound of tanks, appearing for the first time in Somalia, breaks the silence. The Italian army was originally concentrated in the east, north, and south of Abyssinia. However, ships are constantly shuttling, still transporting troops across the Mediterranean to the war zone. The Abyssinian Emperor's Imperial Guard, trained by Europeans, is currently defending the main road from the Abyssinian capital to prevent enemy invasion. The major battle has not yet erupted. According to the Roman public report, only five Italian soldiers and forty Italian colonial troops have been killed. Approximately 180,000 Italian troops are stationed in a fifty-mile wide and twenty-mile deep position in Tigre, northern Abyssinia, currently engaged in consolidating defenses, building roads, and digging wells. They may not advance until November. The Italian army is facing off against three Abyssinian armies, but there has been no contact. Italian newspapers report daily on the surrender of Abyssinian chieftains, and state that General De Bono, the commander-in-chief, has incorporated the entire region of Tigre into Italian territory. (Reuters Telegram, 26th)

(Paris) The Abyssinian Emperor delivered a speech yesterday afternoon in the capital of his country. After being broadcast by the Paris Evening News, people here were able to hear the Emperor's words, which stated, "Since the Italian army launched an offensive against our country's northern and southern borders on October 3rd, the war on the front lines, although once calm, has now resumed its advance. Ten areas of our country are now being ravaged, and our army has no choice but to rise up and resist the enemy to defend ourselves. Our country has always been willing to treat friendly nations with friendship. This war was not initiated by us, as the world can attest. Now, to defend our territory, we are compelled to take up arms against the enemy, for this is our only right." (Havas Telegram, 26th)

(Rome) The Ministry of War today exaggerated the news of the Abyssinian army under General Seyoum attacking the right flank of the Italian army near Aksum, stating that two battalions of artillery should be dispatched to repel this enemy force. The telegram received by the Ministry of War praised the bravery of General Seyoum's troops. (National Telegram, 25th)

Adi-Grar, within a week, or next Monday, which is the thirteenth anniversary of the Fascist Party's march on Rome, the Italian army will launch a major offensive against Maqale. This theory is gaining traction today. The road from here to the front lines is filled day and night with vehicles carrying ammunition and military supplies. Donkeys carrying water bladders are also constantly on the move. Huge artillery vehicles rumble along the rugged roads, raising dust wherever they go. The Associated Press correspondent accompanying the Italian army in the north witnessed workers of all races building roads everywhere. The general public here believes that this offensive will be part of a full-scale general offensive. (National Telegram, 25th)

Abyssinian Capital, it has been learned here that the Abyssinian army in the north, led by General Seyoum, the governor of Tigray Province, attacked the right flank of the Italian army near Aksum today, but was eventually repelled by the Italian artillery. (National Telegram, 25th)

Abyssinian Capital, Special Correspondent O'Chiara reports, according to official announcements, a large Italian force, covered by bombers, occupied two Abyssinian outposts on October 10th, one along the Webi Shebelle River and the other in the town of Qarafa in the Wogga Dahn area. The Abyssinian army was forced to retreat. On October 18th, four Italian aircraft flew over Gora Hai and later bombed the town of Khelit Hapu. (Havas Telegram, 25th)

Abyssinian Capital, the Abyssinian Emperor has now decided to engage the enemy in a decisive battle in the Taysi area. The Hurgas Kompites and Asmara Wan tribal peoples, who have been feuding for centuries, have also joined forces and are heading to the front lines. It is reported that 70,000 cavalrymen are concentrated near Taysi. General Seyoum, General Kessan, and Minister of War General Getachew are deploying a large number of troops. A government spokesman announced here today that although reconciliation efforts are underway in Europe regarding the Abyssinian-Italian dispute, the Abyssinian people intend to expel the Italian army after their troops are concentrated. (National Telegram, 25th)

Abyssinian Capital Radio Station Triples Profits; Monthly Revenue Reaches One Million Francs 20

Abyssinian Capital, Special Correspondent O'Chiara reports, the Abyssinian national radio broadcasting station is now a major source of revenue for the Abyssinian government. Since the outbreak of hostilities, journalists from all over the world have gathered in the Abyssinian capital, all using the radio station to transmit news. Revenue from telegram fees has reached a staggering one million francs per month. The Abyssinian national radio broadcasting station was founded in 1930 and was originally run by Italian merchants. Later, the Abyssinian government, fearing that the only means of communication with the outside world would be monopolized by Italy, secretly signed contracts with a Swedish engineer and a French engineer to build another radio station. Although this radio station has very little power, it is still sufficient. At the beginning of this year, the radio station run by the Italian merchants abandoned competitive operations. Thus, they rely on the new radio station as the only means of communication with the outside world. Since the outbreak of war, the daily transmission volume has increased from 500 words to 100,000 words. There are now three radio stations operating simultaneously in the capital, and ten radio stations are distributed in various Abyssinian military strongholds. The equipment used by each radio station is made in France, and the technicians are all Abyssinian, trained in the capital by foreign engineers. (Havas Telegram, 26th)

British Labour Party Manifesto Advocates Collective Peace; Demands Prompt Action from the League of Nations 21

(London) The Labour Party issued its election manifesto last night, stating that the Labour Party now seeks to sincerely cooperate with the League of Nations and all countries outside the League that desire peace. The Labour Party firmly supports the collective peace system and demands prompt action from the League of Nations to end the war in Africa, and then immediately continue negotiations on disarmament among all countries. However, the Labour Party advocates fully maintaining national defense forces, limited to what is necessary and required by the obligations of a member state of the League of Nations. (Reuters Telegram, 26th)

Herriot Strongly Advocates Fulfilling League of Nations Covenant; French People Should Completely Trust Britain 22

(Paris) Édouard Herriot, the president of the Radical Socialist Party and a non-cabinet minister, recently delivered a speech at the Radical Socialist Party Congress, stating, "France, by virtue of its responsibility and honor, has the necessity to implement the League of Nations Covenant. Britain opposed signing the 1924 Geneva Protocol on Collective Security ten years ago, and its tacit agreement to create collective sanctions is something that our France should be pleased with. Some people criticize Britain's attitude towards the Abyssinian crisis, but it should be known that we should not underestimate Britain's efforts. The British hate lies the most. Now that the British have claimed that they are completely maintaining the League of Nations Covenant in the current dispute and do not have any selfish motives, then we should believe them. British cabinet ministers or gentlemen have always valued integrity, and we should not doubt them. Since British cabinet members have declared 'We stand on this,' then we should completely trust them and not suspect that they have other motives. The real focus of the current issue is not pro-Italy or anti-Italy, nor is it pro-Britain or anti-Britain, but whether we support the League of Nations or oppose the League of Nations." (Havas Telegram, 25th)

Italy's Six Conditions; British Government is Considering Them; Abyssinia States it Will Not Cede an Inch of Territory; League of Nations Sanctions Proceed as Planned 23

(Paris) It has been learned from reliable sources today that Britain and France have received Mussolini's minimum demands for resolving the Abyssinian-Italian war, the contents of which greatly undermine Abyssinian sovereignty and are difficult for Britain and France to recognize. (National News Agency Telegram, 25th)

(London) French Prime Minister Laval has today notified the British government of the Italian tentative suggestions for resolving the Abyssinian-Italian dispute. The contents have not been disclosed by official sources, but Britain's attitude remains unchanged, only reiterating that the British government is always prepared to consider peace proposals, but has never attempted and will never attempt to proceed outside the League of Nations. (Reuters Telegram, 26th)

(Paris) Prime Minister and Foreign Minister Laval met with British Ambassador to France Sir Clerk this morning. Officials are unwilling to comment on the meeting, but say that Laval does not advocate delaying the implementation of the financial and economic sanctions against Italy decided by the League of Nations Assembly Sanctions Committee. (Havas Telegram, 26th)

(London) It has recently been reported that Italian Prime Minister Mussolini has submitted new proposals to French Prime Minister Laval for resolving the Abyssinian-Italian dispute, which Laval has notified to British Ambassador to France Sir Clerk. Although this news was denied by the French Foreign Ministry a few days ago, according to The Times, Britain and France have indeed exchanged views on the Abyssinian-Italian dispute. The newspaper reported, "The French government had inquired with Italian Prime Minister Mussolini about what conditions he would use as a basis for negotiations, and then received a reply from Italy, which was then forwarded to London by Sir Clerk. The British government is currently considering Italy's proposals, and when the appropriate time comes, it will express its views to Laval and make various suggestions. As for Italy's proposals, we can assert that they will not be accepted by the League of Nations, Britain, France, and the Abyssinian Emperor." According to The Times, Mussolini's proposals consist of six points as follows:

(1) Divide Abyssinia into two parts: the mainland territory and the areas inhabited by non-Amharic ethnic groups.

(2) The areas inhabited by non-Amharic ethnic groups should be placed under Italian control in the form of a League of Nations mandate or lease.

(3) The Abyssinian chieftains, clergy, and people of Tigray Province have already recognized Italian sovereignty, and this should be recognized as a fait accompli.

(4) Abyssinian armaments should be effectively monitored to ensure the security of Italian territories in East Africa.

(5) Regarding slavery and other outdated customs, the League of Nations should be responsible for urging Abyssinia to comply with the obligations stipulated in the League of Nations Covenant.

(6) Abyssinia can use the port of Asab in Italian Eritrea as a free port. (Havas Telegram, 26th)

(Paris) Prime Minister and Foreign Minister Laval met with the Italian Ambassador to France, Cerutti, today for a long discussion. (Havas Telegram, 25th)

Abyssinian Capital, an Abyssinian official told a Reuters reporter today that if the Italian army occupies one square inch of Tigray land, there will be no chance of peace. If the Abyssinian Emperor agrees to cede Tigray to the Italians, he will lose his throne within 24 hours. Even financial compensation or access to the sea will not appease the Abyssinian people. (Reuters Telegram, 25th)

(London) Eden is scheduled to go to Geneva on October 30th to attend the League of Nations Sanctions Adjustment Committee the following day to consider the governments' responses regarding the implementation of financial and economic sanctions against Italy. Hopes that the Abyssinian-Italian war may be resolved before the implementation of the pressure plan on Italy seem unlikely to be realized. These hopes are mostly based on the exchange of views between France and Italy, but it is not yet known what the nature of any suggestions exchanged. The League of Nations may not delay the date of implementation of economic sanctions because of this. Responsible parties here all feel that there is no other way than to proceed in Geneva with the plan that has already been agreed upon in principle, as this is the best way to prompt the Abyssinian-Italian dispute to be resolved as soon as possible on terms acceptable to Italy, Abyssinia, and the League of Nations. (Reuters Telegram, 26th)

Italy's New Proposals Will Be Submitted to the Five-Nation Committee; Geneva to Be Active Again in the Middle of Next Week 24

(Paris) Le Petit Parisien reported that the new proposals for resolving the Abyssinian-Italian dispute put forward by the Italian Prime Minister will likely be submitted to the Special Committee of Five Nations of the League of Nations Council for review. The Five-Nation Committee ceased its work after its proposal of September 18 was rejected by Italy. However, the League of Nations has assured that if new proposals are put forward, the committee will continue to meet. The newspaper also believes that the League of Nations Sanctions Scheme Adjustment Committee is scheduled to convene on October 31st, so diplomatic activity in Geneva will greatly develop in the middle of next week. It is reported that British Foreign Secretary Hoare intends to go to Geneva in person at that time, and French Prime Minister and Foreign Minister Laval may also participate in the League of Nations' work if necessary, as not only the implementation of economic sanctions needs to be discussed, but other major issues also need to be dealt with together. (Havas Telegram, 26th)

(Geneva) The League of Nations Secretariat has not received any notification regarding the conditions for resolving the Abyssinian-Italian dispute. However, it is reported that League of Nations Secretary-General Avenol, when he went to London to attend the funeral of the late Chairman of the Disarmament Conference Henderson, discussed the possibility of continued progress in negotiations with the British government. If a solution to the Abyssinian-Italian dispute is to be found within the League of Nations framework, then the cessation of war should be its prerequisite, which is highly valued by League of Nations officials. According to well-informed sources, negotiations to resolve the Abyssinian-Italian dispute will likely still be handled by the League of Nations Council, but the Council will entrust the Five-Nation Committee to be responsible for finding the basis for an agreement. (Havas Telegram, 25th)

Twenty-Eight Countries Have Implemented the Blockade of Military Supplies to Italy; Our Country's Measures Have Been Determined; Britain to Implement from the 29th 25

(Geneva) The League of Nations Secretariat announced today that 28 countries have now implemented a blockade of the transport of military equipment and munitions to Italy, nine countries have already implemented financial sanctions, three countries have expressed their willingness to boycott all Italian goods and prohibit the transport of key items to Italy, and two countries have accepted the principle of economic mutual assistance among countries implementing sanctions. (National Telegram, 25th)

(London) The Privy Council met today and approved the order to implement economic sanctions against Italy, but the date of implementation of the sanctions will depend on the decision of the League of Nations Sanctions Committee. (National Telegram, 26th)

(London) The Treasury issued an order today setting October 29 as the date on which Britain will begin implementing financial sanctions against Italy. From that date onwards, all lending to Italy will be prohibited. It is expected that October 29 will be adopted by other financial centers around the world, so that collective action can have the fullest possible effect. It is reported that the Sanctions Adjustment Committee will meet in Geneva on October 31 to decide on the date for the implementation of economic sanctions against Italy. (Reuters Telegram, 26th)

(London) Today's London Gazette supplement contains the order passed by yesterday's Privy Council to implement sanctions against Italy. The goods prohibited from being exported to Italy are military aircraft, explosives, various raw materials such as metals and rubber, and animals such as mules and camels. Lending to Italy is also prohibited. However, the implementation of financial sanctions must await the decision of the Treasury. The order issued today concerns prohibited items for export to Italy, but gold and silver coins are not included. This ban will apply to certain British territories, protectorates, and mandated territories. (Reuters Telegram, 26th)

Canberra, Prime Minister Lyons notified the League of Nations Secretariat today that the Australian Federation will implement sanctions against Italy in accordance with the dates prescribed by the League of Nations. (National Telegram, 25th)

(Geneva) The governments of Spain and Chile today notified the League of Nations Secretariat that they have followed the resolutions of the League of Nations Assembly Sanctions Committee and prohibited the transportation of military supplies to Italy. (Havas Telegram, 25th)

Capital of Argentina, the government issued an order yesterday afternoon prohibiting arms merchants from trading with Italy and its territories, and from transporting military supplies and ammunition to those locations. (Havas Telegram, 25th)

(Nanjing) Diplomatic circles have learned that the issue of implementing League of Nations sanctions against Italy has been appropriately resolved by our side and will be officially announced soon. External reports regarding the arms embargo are inaccurate, as we have notified the League of Nations. (Special Dispatch, 26th)

On the Issue of Sanctions Against Italy, the United States Will Give an Official Reply to the League of Nations; Wording is Euphemistic and Does Not Make Direct Expressions; Only States That Maintaining Peace Remains Its Original Intention 26

(Washington) The State Department will today give an official reply to the League of Nations regarding the United States' actions on the Abyssinian-Italian dispute and its general relationship with world peace. According to well-informed sources, the United States will not announce straightforward opinions. The wording of the reply will be euphemistic and leave the League of Nations to draw its own conclusions. The United States' reply will list the following facts: (1) The Abyssinian Emperor invoked the Pact of Paris on June 3; (2) Secretary of State Hull's warning to the Italian Ambassador that the United States had deep misgivings about Italian actions that might lead to war; (3) President Roosevelt's arms embargo order. Officials declared that the United States' arms embargo is a powerful expression of support for peace, so there will be no further action at present. (National Telegram, 26th)

(Washington) President Roosevelt recently made a statement to the press, stating, "The government will send out a reply soon after receiving the League of Nations' note on the implementation of sanctions against Italy. The attitude of the United States in its reply regarding the issue of sanctions will be based on the provisions of the neutrality laws, as the neutrality laws do not permit the government to take the same sanctions as the League of Nations." When asked whether the United States was prepared to prohibit the transport of gasoline and copper to belligerent countries, the President replied that if necessary, it would be considered. Asked about the naval shipbuilding issue, Roosevelt replied that he had not ordered the construction of new ships, as the United States' main battleships could only be replaced after the Washington Treaty expires in 1937 in accordance with treaty provisions. (Havas Telegram, 25th)

(Washington) Former Secretary of State Stimson of the Hoover administration met with current Secretary of State Hull for an hour today to discuss the League of Nations' request for the United States' views on the implementation of economic sanctions against Italy. Stimson's visit to Hull has caused much speculation here. Some observers believe that this conversation indicates that the government is now trying to avoid attacks from the opposition party on the government's policies toward the European situation. It is known that Stimson's trip to the State Department was at Hull's invitation. Stimson recently expressed his dissatisfaction that the United States had failed to cooperate with the League of Nations in dealing with the Abyssinian-Italian war. However, the stated purpose of this visit is related to the upcoming horse race in the United States, which Stimson is very interested in. American disarmament representative Davis also met with Hull and President Roosevelt one after another today. (National Telegram, 25th)

British Election Campaign Begins; Baldwin's Speech; The League of Nations Still Faces More Serious Tests; Military Blockade May Be Inevitable 27

(London) Prime Minister Baldwin gave his first election campaign broadcast speech tonight, stating that if all countries joined the League of Nations, then war could be prevented. Now that Germany, Japan, and the United States are outside the League of Nations, preventing war has become even more difficult. Under these circumstances, it is also expected that the League of Nations will encounter a period of testing, and the League of Nations may still have more serious tests in the future. If it is necessary to implement severe sanctions, then a blockade will ultimately be inevitable. This difficult responsibility will initially fall on the British Navy, and hopefully, it will be shared with the navies of other countries. If not, then it may have to be borne alone. Britain has led the world toward disarmament, but other countries have not followed suit, and have instead expanded their armaments, not only expanding them but also modernizing them. Moreover, several countries have increased their armaments to an enormous extent. We do not want to have a huge military force, but we want to modernize our armaments. The world should know that after the European War, Britain only built three main battleships, and the construction models of the remaining ships were all designed before attention had to be paid to aerial attacks. Britain's cruisers are mostly outdated and unsuitable for use in the new era. If I do not have the power to remedy the deficiencies in our national defense after the European War, then I cannot be responsible for the government's actions. We do not need a huge military force, but we must ensure that all our weapons are the most advanced in the world.

(London) The decree dissolving the current Parliament and convening a new Parliament on November 26 has been published in last night's London Gazette supplement. The headquarters of the various parties are now busy arranging campaign speeches for their party leaders, nominating candidates, and sending election materials to the various constituencies. There are a total of 615 seats in the House of Commons, and there are now as many as 1,270 candidates. The coalition parties have 563 candidates, including 498 from the Conservative Party, 42 from the National Liberal Party, 20 from the National Labour Party, and 3 from the "National Party." The opposition parties have a total of 710 candidates, including 530 from the Labour Party, 150 from the Liberal Party, and 30 from the Independent Labour Party. Sixty-two current members of the House of Commons do not wish to seek re-election, including 55 from the Conservative Party, including Countess Iveagh, Secretary of State for Scotland and Minister of the Navy Monsell, and Scottish Solicitor General Jamieson have been appointed as judges. The manifestos of the various parties have been published one after another. The Labour Party is appealing to voters to follow a fixed socialist direction. The Communist Party supports the restoration of the Labour Party government. The "National Unity" Party manifesto, signed by Baldwin, MacDonald, and Simon, will be published soon. Samuel advised his party members to vote in constituencies without "Samuel Liberal Party" candidates for candidates who support Lloyd George's policy of establishing a National Peace and Reconstruction Conference. Lloyd George gave a speech in Caernarfon today, criticizing the government for using the opposition parties' differences of opinion on the East African war to hold a general election, saying that Baldwin knew that there was no chance of a socialist government at this time, and that the danger of a "rascally majority" was even greater. (Reuters Telegram, 26th)

(Washington) Since the Senate Silver Investigation Committee convened in Salt Lake City, silver experts believe that whether the issue of bimetallism can be raised in the 1936 general election depends on Senator Borah alone. Recent developments prove that Committee Chairman Pittman and other leaders who drafted the 1932 Democratic platform unanimously believe that the government's silver policy is satisfactory. At the same time, Senator Thomas has indeed expressed dissatisfaction with the government's policy. However, there is now a trend to promote managed currency. Some other silver senators, in order to pass the veterans' benefits bill in the next parliament, will probably advocate a paper money inflation policy. Conservatives within the Republican Party can hardly be expected to support the price ratio of sixteen to one for gold and silver. Therefore, if no Western senator with national renown comes forward to fight for it, the issue of bimetallism will likely fade into obscurity. Borah is clearly the only figure with the ability to attract national attention to the silver issue. Most recently, Borah has been evasive about the silver issue for some reason. (Washington) Experts today declared that the stagnation of the world silver market has led merchants with excessive stockpiles to sell abroad, thus contributing to the drastic fall in the price of Chinese currency. It has long been believed here that the Treasury would not accelerate the purchase of silver without pressure from the silver faction in Congress. However, the silver faction is very depressed because Congress is currently in recess. It is believed here that the reason for the drastic fall in the price of Chinese currency is that the general public cannot grasp the future currency policy of the Chinese government. (25th Kuomintang News Agency Dispatch)

(New York) The reason for the rise in silver prices in the New York market has not yet been announced. Experts today told the Associated Press that China will eventually recover the silver purchased by the United States, and the price it pays per ounce will not exceed US$0.35. However, this will happen ten or fifteen years later. (25th Kuomintang News Agency Dispatch)

Even the current daily exchange of mail is only over 30,000, a significant decrease from before. (26th Special Dispatch)

After the Breach of the Salt River; Northern Guanyun City Submerged 37

(Xuzhou) After the eastern bank of the Salt River breached, the breach was too large and could not be blocked. The waves surged and poured into the northeast. Two hundred square li north of Guanyun County was completely submerged. All the roads outside the city leading to Xinpu rely on boat transportation. County Magistrate Xu has now retreated to the county seat, supervising the civilians to surround and fortify the city walls. The embankment on the east bank of the Salt River south of the county seat is also in great danger. The salt transport commissioner has hired civilians and transferred salt farmers from the east bank to protect the east embankment to protect 10,000 hectares of salt fields. In addition, the Salt Affairs Inspection Office has temporarily moved to the county party headquarters in Banpu City. (26th Central News Agency Dispatch)

(Xuzhou) After Guanyun City was surrounded by water, the urban area was busy repairing the city embankments and rushing to build up the Salt River embankment. All four rural areas were flooded, and traffic was cut off, making it impossible to set up defenses. Many bandit ships were discovered, taking advantage of the flood to loot, kidnapping people, stealing cattle, and plundering food, one after another. Because there are many refugees entering the city to escape the disaster, the county government is intensifying its defenses due to the complexity of the population. (26th Special Dispatch)

The People of Feng and Pei Counties; Still Strictly Defending 38

(Xuzhou) Pei News After the breach of the Gaoxiao Huxi Embankment, County Magistrate Yang Guozhen is leading the people to rush to plug the breach. The weather cleared up today, and the lake water has receded since yesterday. The momentum of the breach has subsided, and the city of Pei should be safe. The northern embankment of Feng County has not been in danger and is still peaceful. However, the people of the two counties are still strictly defending. (26th Special Dispatch)

Hubei Province Decides to Repair the Jianghan Embankment; By Enlisting the People's Service 39

(Hankou) The provincial government decided to repair the Jianghan Embankment by enlisting the people's service. It has designated 22 embankments, with 100,000 people starting construction, and planting 2 million trees along the embankment. The Flood Relief General Association decided to expand the winter emergency relief and allocate winter clothing. (26th Special Dispatch)

(Hankou) Xi Dejiong, Director of the Jianghan Engineering Bureau, recently inspected the three or four breaches in the upper reaches of the Xiang River. On the evening of the 26th, he took the Jianghua Ship to Jinling (Nanjing) to report to the Economic Committee and to negotiate everything. (26th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Economic Commission Continues to Allocate; The Remaining Funds for Dongzhuang Breach Plugging 40

(Nanjing) The Lu Province requested the allocation of the remaining funds for the Dongzhuang breach. The Economic Commission has now allocated 200,000 yuan to be remitted to the Central Bank. (26th Special Dispatch)

(Nanjing) Kong Xiangrong, Deputy Chairman of the Yellow River Flood Relief Commission, returned to Jinling from Shanghai on the 26th and is scheduled to return to Bian on the 27th. (26th Special Dispatch)

(Kaifeng) Liu Bingzhong, Director of Inspection for Flood Prevention, reported back after inspecting the water situation and engineering of the Dongzhuang breach, stating: 1. A new embankment should be built after the Jiangyun Dam, but construction has not yet begun; 2. The top of the Jiangyun Dam is slightly slow; 3. Three sections of the Lisheng Tun revetment dingxiang sweeping have collapsed; 4. The breach at the southern end of Gengnian is more than 130 zhang wide; 5. There are currently 1,600 cubic meters of stone and construction materials in stock. (26th Special Dispatch)

International Commercial Telegram October 26th Reuters Special Commercial News 88

Gold and Silver

London gold price fell half a penny today to one hundred and forty-one shillings and six pence.

London Silver Market The price remained unchanged today, with spot at twenty-nine pence three one two five, and futures at twenty-nine pence one eight seven five. The market is stable, with purchases from the United States and India, and sales from China.

Exchange Rates

British-American The London foreign exchange market was quiet this morning. The British-American exchange rate opened this morning at four dollars, nine cents, one point five six two five, lower than yesterday's closing rate for American-British exchange by zero six two five. After an hour, it fell another one two five, but the closing price recovered to the same as the opening price.

British-French The opening price was one pound higher, at seventy-four francs, fifty-four. It continued to rise three pounds at 11:00 AM, but fell back to seventy-four francs, fifty-four at closing.

Cotton and Wheat

New York Cotton Market The opening this morning was flat, but trading was quiet. Near-term prices rose slightly, while far-term prices initially plummeted, then recovered, with some spread buying. However, demand was good, especially from overseas, so short selling was absorbed.

Liverpool Cotton The market was relatively stable this morning. The closing price for January futures was 6.11, up two pounds.

Chicago Wheat The opening this morning plummeted. The price for December futures fell six two five, due to short selling pressure. The opening price for mixed grains fell one two five, and trading was sluggish.

Liverpool Wheat Prices fell slightly today. The closing price for December futures was six shillings, four pence, three seven five, down two five.

Rubber

London The opening was firm this morning. The transaction price for January-March futures was six pence, six two five, higher than yesterday's price by zero six two five. The price remained unchanged at noon.

New York The opening price fell five pounds today due to profit-taking at the end of the week, but sentiment was still good, and the decline ended after the fall.

Securities

New York Securities opened this morning with uniform price increases, except for a slight decline in film stocks. Sentiment was strong, and profit-taking continued unabated. Steel stocks rose the most. The Dow Jones 30 industrial stock average opened at one hundred forty-one shillings, up thirty-one pounds. The New York stock market prices are listed on the left.

Yellow River Closure Project Likely to Halt 90

Due to Central Government Funds Not Yet Remitted for the Closure Project

Jinan Correspondence: The Dongzhuang Yellow River project in Shandong is vast. According to the Dongzhuang meeting's decision principles, the closure committee estimated the construction plan and budgeted over 4.8 million yuan. The closure project alone requires over 1.3 million yuan. Regarding the construction funds, the central government has only remitted 300,000 yuan for disaster relief, leaving only 240,000 yuan. Han Fuqu, chairman of the Shandong Provincial Government, repeatedly requested to be relieved of the responsibility for the closure. The committee replied, urging him to persevere and promising to continue allocating 1 million yuan in construction funds, starting with 300,000 yuan. A total of 540,000 yuan has been received so far, plus 100,000 yuan in assistance from the Jiangsu Provincial Government, totaling 640,000 yuan. Zhang Honglie, Director of the Shandong Construction Department, was appointed as the chairman of the closure committee, leading the staff to actively prepare for the closure project, purchasing materials, and intensifying transportation. The Li Jingtun remnant revetment head and the extension of the Jiangsu Dam, and the construction of a diversion dam and other projects, started successively on the 15th and 20th of this month. They are currently working hard to complete the foundations of the east and west dams, and after the ice flood, they will take the opportunity to close the breach. However, the construction funds received for purchasing materials have long been exhausted. Now that the project continues to advance, funds are urgently needed. According to Zhou Li, director of the construction team, the purchase of materials requires 1,934,973.45 yuan. The bidding has been completed, and over 721,000 yuan must be paid before November 1st. After the closure committee submitted a report to Chairman Han Fuqu, Han has sent three telegrams in succession, urging the Economic Commission to remit the 700,000 yuan of the promised million yuan as soon as possible to meet the urgent needs. However, there has been no response to date. It is estimated that if the construction funds do not arrive in the next few days, the closure project will inevitably come to a standstill. According to Zhang Honglie, chairman of the closure committee, if the construction funds are not remitted within days, he will not be able to be responsible for the closure and will immediately submit his resignation, requesting that another capable person be appointed to replace him. It is also heard that Zhang has sent telegrams to Qin Fen, Secretary-General of the Economic Commission, and Kong Xiangrong, acting chairman of the Yellow River Conservancy Commission, stating this opinion. (24th)

Difficult to Repair the Breach in the Upper Reaches of the Xiang River 91

The breach in the No. 34 Levee extends for four to five kilometers.

The construction of a remote levee requires 80,000 laborers per day and will take five months to complete.

Xi Dejiong goes to Nanjing again to discuss the start of construction with the Economic Commission.

Hankou Correspondence: Regarding the repair of the breach in the main Jiang-Xiang levee, the Jianghan Engineering Bureau previously convened a meeting and decided on a plan and steps to implement. First, work will start on the Zhongxiang No. 24 Levee on the Xiang River line, followed by the No. 11 Levee, and then the levees on the Yangtze River line. The No. 34 Levee suffered the most damage, and its location in the upper reaches is of great importance, so it is necessary to build it in advance. Xi Dejiong, Director of the Jianghan Engineering Bureau, went to the upper reaches of the Xiang River on the 20th by boat for a personal inspection for the sake of careful engineering, and returned to Hankou on the 25th. According to Xi, he arrived at Jiukou on the 22nd and landed on the 23rd to inspect the proposed levee line and the No. 34 Levee breach. From Jiukou via Shagang to Luojiaji Luohansi and then via Guanyintang Zhengjiaji to the No. 34 Levee breach mouth, the journey is over 70 li. Along the way, the villages passed through, after the great flood, mostly became ruins. The corpses of people and animals, doors, tables, chairs, and other objects washed away by the flood could be seen everywhere. From Zhengjiaji to the mouth of the No. 34 Levee breach, more than ten li is a stretch of sand, as if in the desert. The tragic situation of this year's flood and the severity of the damage can be imagined. The No. 34 Levee is located in the upper reaches of the Xiang River, commanding a high position. After the levee broke, the water flowed westward, affecting more than ten counties in the lower reaches of northern Hubei. The mouth is as wide as four or five kilometers. Looking at the south of the breach from afar, it forms a semi-circular shape with a stretch of sand in the south half. The water flowing from the north overflows, and there are more than ten breaches below, such as the No. 11 Levee, with the disaster being concentrated in one corner. The breach is so huge, that compared to the great disaster of the 20th year of the Republic and the Yellow River breaches over the years, it is even more severe. The restoration is not only a matter of hope for the post-disaster refugees, but also a concern for the people of the whole country. Those who care about levee policy know its importance. Although the restoration plan has been discussed and decided, with the construction of a remote levee as the principle, the location of the breach and interruption of flow still needs to be selected and compared. A survey team has been dispatched to conduct detailed surveys of the nearby terrain before a decision is made. The remote levee project at that location is approximately 18 kilometers long and requires more than 2 million cubic meters of earth. The average height of the levee body reaches more than 10 meters. It is planned to start construction in early November and be completed in March next year. On average, more than 80,000 workers are required every day. After construction starts, they will gather in one corner, plus the people involved, military police, and merchants, the number will reach more than 100,000. Taking food as an example, more than 1,000 dan of relief are needed every day to meet the supply. From this one aspect, one can imagine how huge the project is. In the 10th year of the Republic, E Shen Li Yinchen supervised the Wangjiaying closure project, possessing the special power to command the military and civilians of the entire province. It took more than eight months to complete. The current remote levee project is two-thirds larger than the Wangjiaying project, and the construction time is shorter, so the assistance of local people is needed to avoid delaying the work. Xi is scheduled to report to the provincial government on the 20th about the inspection, and will go to Nanjing again within days to report to the three standing committee members of the Economic Commission and Secretary-General Qin to discuss the progress. In any case, construction can start in early November. (25th)

Changzhou Major Theft from Bank Safe Deposit Boxes

Since the opening of the Yixing branch of the Wujin Bank on April 1st of this year, the business has been relatively developed. At about 3:00 AM on the 24th of this month, the branch manager Tan Liangxi heard faint noises from the vault while sleeping. He thought it was rats or insects and did not suspect anything else. When he woke up in the morning and asked the servant Zhou Jinsheng to check, the door to the vault was already wide open. He rushed to inspect and saw that the safe deposit boxes had been damaged. The cash and silver dollars stored in the boxes, totaling 4,000 yuan, 490 yuan in fractional currency, plus 15 yuan in loose silver dollars, and 138 pieces of jewelry (weighing over fifty taels) were completely stolen, with a loss of approximately ten thousand yuan. A bowl of clean water containing iron rust was found under the boxes. Manager Tan, considering the seriousness of the matter, immediately reported to the Wujin headquarters by telephone. Deputy Manager Li Xing also went to Yixing by car to investigate the incident and reported it to the Yixing Public Security Bureau for investigation. According to news on the 25th, over 490 yuan in fractional currency and envelopes containing jewelry were found in a bamboo basket in the branch's kitchen, as well as a steel spiral drill with an arrow shape, with English words engraved on the drill. The servant Zhou Jinsheng, Little Sanzi, and the cook Lu Genbao, who were considered highly suspicious, were all sent to the Public Security Bureau for temporary custody.

Wuxi Telegraphic Request to Correct the Occupation of the Confucian Temple

The Wuxi County Education Bureau has been renting part of the old Fourth Township Office as its office for more than ten years. Starting last year, the county funds purchased a base behind the county court and deposited over 10,000 yuan for the construction of houses. Recently, after the new Director of Education Hui Meishan took office, he proposed to move the bureau and advocated that there was no need to build houses and that the saved construction funds should be used for other purposes. It was proposed and discussed at the first bureau affairs meeting, and it was decided to repair the houses in the two wings of the History Museum originally located in the Confucian Temple, and add straw houses to the front and rear gaps as the office location of the bureau. The original items stored in the museum were collected and stored in the Dacheng Hall for safekeeping. It was also submitted to the County Government Affairs Conference, and it was resolved that the Education Bureau and the Construction Bureau would send personnel to estimate the budget and bidding methods and submit them for approval. More than ten local gentry, including Hua Wenchuan and Gao Xiang, believe that the county bureau's actions clearly violate the National Government and Chairman Chiang's repeated orders to protect and worship the Confucian Temple, and the regulations of the Internal Affairs, Finance, and Education ministries on the management of Confucian Temple property. They jointly telegraphed the National Government, Chairman Chiang, the Jiangsu Provincial Government, and the Ministry of Civil Affairs and the Ministry of Education, requesting that they be clearly ordered to correct the situation and immediately dismiss the proposal to prevent absurdities. The Second Township Office in that location also moved into the Confucian Temple's Sage Shrine to conduct business without permission, and requested that the district chief of that district be severely punished to serve as a warning to those who defy the sages and laws.

Bengbu Transport Department Orders Maintenance of Salt Rotation System

Bengbu is the only large salt market in northern Anhui. Its source is all transported from the Haizhou Banpu area of ​​northern Jiangsu. Because salt is abundant and the supply exceeds demand, there are occasional situations of rushing to sell it. In order to stabilize the salt market, the Lianghuai Salt Transport Envoy's Office presented a request to the Ministry of Finance in the winter of the 21st year of the Republic, which was approved to implement a rotation sales system. At that time, the Xiaguan Inspection Bureau was notified that all stations in the Jinpei Southern Section except Bengbu and Mingguang were not allowed to release transportation. In order to resist private salt on the Liuan banks, Gu鎮 was opened out of necessity. The intention was originally to protect national taxes and people's food. However, Bengbu's salt must be entered into the warehouse for exchange rotation as a rule. Over time, the cost became heavier. Mingu’s salt is sold as soon as it arrives, with a lighter cost. Therefore, Bengbu's salt prices are difficult to be on par with Mingu. Most frustratingly, a few merchants transported and sold Mingu’s salt in Bengbu and the Hebei area. As a result, the rotation salt system was greatly affected. In order to maintain the Bengbu salt rotation sales system, the Salt Transport Envoy's Office recently telegraphed the tax collection office, ordering that salt, regardless of whether it is transported by vehicle, sea, or river, should be sold on a rotation basis according to its arrival in Bengbu. All salt from Mingguang and Guzhen should be sold at its designated sales bank. If it is transported and sold in Bengbu again, it will be ordered to stop selling it once it is verified.

The End of October is Approaching Soon; the Foundation of the Money Shops is Solid 99

Yesterday's Discussion Focused on Returning the Financial Bonds Ordered by the Ministry of Finance

The Reserve Treasury Has Strong Strength and Will Continue to Roll Over Long-Term Loans

The difficult end of October is approaching soon. The strength of the money shops in this city is unusually strong, so there is no need to worry about a smooth passage. The Ministry of Finance is urging the return of financial bonds, and the money shops have decided to do their best to return them. All long-term loans will be rolled over in accordance with the instructions. A reporter from the Industrial and Commercial News Agency has investigated and reported the following details:

Abundant Funds in the Money Shops

The 55 member shops belonging to the Money Shops Association, mindful of the financial turmoil at the end of April, which affected Shanghai's instability, held a general managers' meeting in the autumn to discuss how to maintain the industry and strengthen its strength in order to prevent problems before they arise. With the added attention of Mr. Qin Xieqing, General Manager of the Reserve Treasury, each shop was instructed to do its best to strengthen its financial reserves to prevent unforeseen circumstances. It is understood that the shops have recently increased their own reserves, with a large amount of deposits, so the reserves in the money shops are unusually abundant.

Returning Government Bonds

In May of this year, the Ministry of Finance allocated 25 million yuan of financial bonds to maintain the foundation of the money shops because of the financial turmoil in Shanghai. Afterwards, the shops have separately returned more than 9 million yuan, leaving more than 16 million yuan outstanding. Now, the Ministry of Finance believes that the money shops are unusually stable, so it has ordered the Money Shops Supervision Committee to send a letter urging the shops to repay the debt, and recommended Commissioner Qin Runqing to contact the association. The association, considering the importance of the matter, convened a meeting of managers and representatives at its office on Ningbo Road at 2:00 yesterday afternoon. More than 30 related shops, including Fuyuan, Zikang, Jintai, Tongrun, Anyu, Ankang, Yida, and Hengxun, attended. Mr. He Zhongxiao chaired the meeting, which lasted for about an hour before adjourning. It is understood that the meeting concluded that the government bonds urged for repayment by the Ministry of Finance would be partially repaid first due to the full rollover of long-term loans at the end of October, and the remaining amount would be repaid after the end of October.

Long-Term Rollover

Most of the long-term industrial and commercial credit loans extended by the member shops of the money shops at the end of October were rolled over at the end of April and should be repaid at the end of this month. However, according to the instructions of the Ministry of Finance, the Shanghai National Products Industry Association has sent a letter requesting further assistance for industrial and commercial development, and it has been decided to follow the ministry's instructions and roll over all long-term loans in order to maintain the original intention of relieving the market. The receipt and disbursement of funds has not been busy in recent days, and the market's foreign exchange rates are very low, at 1.5 cents yesterday morning and afternoon, which proves that the money shops are stable and the demand for funds is not high.

The Shanghai Branch of Guangdong Bank: Bondholders Met Yesterday 100

Agreed to Resume Business; Communicate with Hong Kong Bondholders for Unified Handling

Unanimously Elected Chen Bingqian and Wen Qinfu as Plenipotentiary Representatives

The Guangdong Bank bondholders held a creditors' meeting at the Guang Zhao Public Hall on Ningbo Road at 4:00 yesterday afternoon. More than 100 people, including Wen Qinfu of the Guang Zhao Public Hall, Jiang Tianduo of the Guangdong Fellow Villagers Association, and Chen Bingqian of the Guangdong Overseas Chinese Business Federation, attended. Chen Bingqian was unanimously elected as chairman to report that, according to the resolution of the creditors' meeting on October 14, opinions were solicited from the creditors on the proposal to support the resumption of business or liquidation. So far, replies have been received: 649,833.32 yuan supported the resumption of business, 16,620.08 yuan supported liquidation, and 2,073.93 yuan supported both liquidation and resumption of business. The majority supported the resumption of business, and the creditors were asked to express their opinions in order to proceed. After the chairman's report, the creditors expressed many opinions, and the following resolutions were passed: (1) As the Hong Kong National Bank is registered in Hong Kong, the Hong Kong government should be requested to allow the creditors to manage the debts themselves in order to proceed; (2) A letter of support for the resumption of business and a letter of liquidation should be prepared and sent to the Hong Kong bondholders for unified handling; (3) Chen Bingqian and Wen Qinfu were elected as plenipotentiary representatives of the Shanghai branch bondholders and were solely responsible for handling the matter. The meeting adjourned at 6:00 after the discussions.

Tomorrow is the National Day of Czechoslovakia; Czechs Celebrate Joyfully 101

Tomorrow is the 17th anniversary of the independence of the Czechoslovak Republic. Czechs all over the world will celebrate joyfully on this day. Czechoslovakia was established after the end of the European War. In the early years of its founding, enemies believed that this naive country would soon collapse. Later, seeing its national foundation become increasingly solid, they turned to astonishment. As for today, not only does no one envy or slander it, but they are also glad that the Czechoslovak Republic exists, because several neighboring countries rely on Czechoslovakia to be stable. Czechoslovakia is the only country in Central Europe that has not been infected by Bolshevism and the only country that has not depreciated its currency. In recent years, neighboring countries have either implemented a dictatorial system or abolished the parliamentary system. Only Czechoslovakia still maintains Western European democracy in the parliamentary system. Despite the global economic turmoil, its finances are still very stable and its foreign debts have been repaid without any default. In the 17 years since its founding, President Masaryk and Foreign Minister Dr. Beneš have continued to serve together, and their policies have been consistent. This is something that the rest of Europe cannot match. Czechoslovakia's policy focuses on good neighborliness and it is a major member of the Little Entente. The maintenance of peace in Central Europe relies heavily on its efforts, and it supports the League of Nations wholeheartedly. In the 17 years, through hard work, it has achieved today's prosperity, which is all due to the unity of the people from top to bottom, with one heart and one mind.

Promoting the Draft Bill on Acceptance Bills; the Loan Committee Has Revised It 102

Yesterday, Letters Were Sent to the Banking and Money Shops and the Central Bank to Solicit Agreement

After Agreement is Obtained, it Will Be Submitted to the Ministry of Finance for Approval and Implementation

The Industrial and Commercial Loan Review Committee has completed the revision of the draft measures for promoting acceptance bills, which was passed at the 15th meeting. It has sent the revised text to the Banking and Money Shops Association, requesting them to solicit the consent of the lending banks and shops. At the same time, the committee directly sent a letter to the Central Bank to solicit its agreement, because the Central Bank is also one of the lending banks, but not a member of the Banking Association. A reporter from New New News has recorded the original letter and the original draft of the revised measures for promoting acceptance bills as follows:

Soliciting Agreement

The Loan Committee's letter to the Banking and Money Shops Association and the Central Bank stated: "Dear Sirs, it has been three months since the Industrial and Commercial Credit Small Loans allocated by the banking and money industries to our committee for review and release began to be processed. The amount released is only 200,000 yuan, less than one-tenth of the total amount. Our committee, understanding the situation, in order to further assist industry and commerce, encourage production, circulate domestic goods, and maintain the livelihood of workers, has discussed and decided to allocate 3 million yuan from the Industrial and Commercial Credit Small Loans recognized and borrowed by the banks and shops as a fund for promoting industrial and commercial acceptance bills. The draft measures for promoting acceptance bills were passed at the 15th meeting of our committee. Whether the allocation of funds to handle acceptance bills and the draft measures are feasible should be subject to the opinions of the lending banks and shops before being submitted to the Ministry of Finance for approval and implementation. In addition to sending separate letters, we are enclosing a copy of the draft measures and (requesting) that (your bank agree and asking that you check and) (the association solicit the agreement of the lending banks and shops) and reply. In addition, regarding the organization entrusted to handle acceptance bills in Article 2 of the measures, our committee has discussed and proposed that the banks and shops that recognize and allocate small credit loans should be responsible for handling them separately. However, how to entrust the handling, whether to entrust all or part of the banks and shops to handle it, and whether the number of such bills handled by each bank and shop should be limited or unlimited, we hope that (your bank) (association) will check and provide detailed opinions to facilitate implementation. Yours sincerely, (Central Bank) Shanghai (Banking) (Money) Shops Association, Chairman Cai Zengji."

Revised Draft

Draft Measures for Promoting Acceptance Bills by the Shanghai Industrial and Commercial Loan Review Committee: (1) In order to assist industry and commerce, encourage production, circulate domestic goods, and maintain the livelihood of workers, this committee, with the consent of the lending banks and shops, has requested and obtained approval from the Ministry of Finance to allocate 3 million yuan of national currency from the small credit loans as a fund for the acceptance and discount of industrial and commercial bills, and the government bonds allocated by the Ministry will still be used as the second guarantee. (2) The acceptance and discount of these bills shall be handled by the lending banks and shops entrusted by this committee, and all handling fees shall be borne by the applicant. (3) After the entrusted banks and shops submit the above-mentioned bills for review by this committee, the committee shall issue government bond receipts according to the amount as proof of the second guarantee. (4) The methods of acceptance and discount are as follows: (A) If an industrial or commercial enterprise stores raw materials or goods in a warehouse, and they have been identified as needed and valuable in the market and have gone through the transfer procedures, they may fill out a bank acceptance bill at the discount rate prescribed in these measures, and the entrusted bank or shop shall accept it. (B) If an industrial or commercial enterprise holds a commercial acceptance bill obtained from the sale of goods, it may apply to the entrusted bank or shop for discount. If the related parties of the above-mentioned bill have been verified to have considerable financial resources, they may be exempted from providing a guarantee. (C) The face value of the bill requested for acceptance by an industrial or commercial enterprise shall not exceed 60% of the estimated value of the goods provided as collateral for the bill specified in item A, and shall not exceed 5,000 yuan for the bill specified in item B. The term of acceptance of each bill shall not exceed four months. (D) The discount rate for the aforementioned acceptance bills shall be 8% per month. The banks and shops handling the discount shall report the names and amounts of the discounters to the committee daily. (5) When a bank acceptance bill becomes due, the applicant shall pay the full amount to the entrusted bank or shop. If the applicant fails to pay, the entrusted bank or shop may, in addition to making a payment on its behalf, sell the raw materials or goods provided as collateral to offset the payment. If the amount is insufficient, it may also recover the amount from the related parties of the bill. (6) When a commercial acceptance bill becomes due, the acceptor shall pay the full amount. If the acceptor fails to pay, the entrusted bank or shop may, in addition to making a payment on its behalf, recover the amount from the related parties of the bill. (7) The amount of bill acceptance and discount shall be limited to 3 million yuan for the time being. If the applicant has already paid the amount when it becomes due, the committee may continue to handle acceptance and discount within its quota. (8) The entrusted banks and shops may handle the procedures for bill acceptance and discount in accordance with the usual practices of the financial market. (9) In addition to the above provisions, all regulations issued by the Ministry of Finance to this committee shall apply. (10) These measures shall be implemented from the date of approval by the Ministry of Finance.

Shipping Bill of Lading: Stamp Duty Issue Resolved 103

Since the implementation of the new stamp duty regulations in September, the shipping companies in Shanghai have strongly opposed the 20-cent stamp duty on each bill of lading and sent representatives to Beijing to petition for a revision of the tax rate, which has been successfully resolved. This matter is related to shipping and transportation, so it is described in detail as follows:

Requesting Revision

Since September, all shipping merchants in Shanghai have asked the Shanghai Shipping Industry Association to send a telegram to the Legislative Yuan in Nanjing, requesting the revision of the article requiring a 20-cent stamp duty on each bill of lading, because some of the minimum bills of lading for cargo loaded by Shanghai ships only have a freight charge of 50 cents. According to the new stamp duty, the tax amount reaches 40%, which is rare and cannot be borne by the shipping merchants. The Legislative Yuan accepted the petition and agreed to open a finance committee to discuss and deliberate.

Representatives Attending

On the 18th of this month, the Legislative Yuan held a finance meeting to discuss revising the amount of stamp duty on bills of lading in the new stamp duty. The Legislative Yuan specially invited representatives from Shanghai shipping merchants to attend in Beijing for consultation. The shipping merchants in Shanghai unanimously recommended Yuan Ludeng, Wei Wenhan, Wang Zigang, and others to go to Beijing. When the representatives went to Beijing, they provided the Legislative Yuan with the most powerful evidence by providing the smallest bill of lading of the shipping company, which was only 14 cents, for reference.

Satisfactory Resolution

The representatives stated in Beijing that the new stamp duty should change the method of affixing the tax amount to the bill of lading and reduce the tax rate. The Legislative Yuan also adopted this proposal. As a result of the discussion, a very satisfactory solution was reached. It is now agreed that: (1) Domestic cargo bills of lading will not be affixed with stamps, and the stamp duty will be affixed to the customs duty bill; (2) Inland cargo will have the stamp duty affixed to the bill of lading due to tax exemption, and the tax rate is very low; (3) Cargo transported abroad must have stamps affixed to the bill of lading. The representatives achieved their goals and returned to Shanghai.

Marine Loss Expert

Marine loss calculation is a specialized subject, and our country has never had such talent. Whenever an accident occurs, foreign merchants must be asked to handle the calculation of marine losses. Mr. Wei Wenda has personally gone to various countries in Europe and America to study marine losses. Mr. Wei has interned in major insurance companies in Europe and America for many years and has returned to China after completing his studies. Shipping merchants in this port are preparing to hold a meeting to welcome him. In the future, if Chinese ships have maritime accidents, the calculation of marine losses can be entrusted to domestic experts instead of relying on foreigners.
